        e.preventDefault();
        jQuery('body').removeClass('has_alerts');

        var d = new Date(),
            now = Math.floor(d.getTime()/1000),
            futureMath = 0 - now,
            futureTime = d.setTime(now + futureMath),
            exdate = new Date((futureTime * 1000));

    <div class="inner">
     <span class="title">
      Cancer Risk Reduction
     </span>
     <p>
     </p>
     <p>
      Take our Cancer Prevention Quiz to test your knowledge and learn more about cancer risk factors and risk reduction.
     </p>
     <a class="btn white tall wide" href="https://aacr.org/Pages/CancerPreventionQuiz/">
      Take the Quiz
     </a>
    </div>
   </div>

  <section class="by-the-numbers">
   <div class="container">
    <span class="section-title">
     By the Numbers
    </span>
    <div class="the-numbers">
     <div class="num">
      <div class="inner">
       <span class="title">
        16.9
       </span>
       <p>
        million cancer survivors in the U.S. are living with, through, and beyond their disease thanks to research
       </p>
       <a class="link" href="https://cancerprogressreport.aacr.org/progress/cpr20-contents/cpr20-cancer-in-2020//?utm_source=aacr-org&amp;utm_medium=bynumbers&amp;utm_campaign=cpr#driving%20">
        Learn More
       </a>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="num">
      <div class="inner">
       <span class="title">
        4 in 10
       </span>
       <p>
        cancer diagnoses in the United States are associated with preventable risk factors
       </p>
       <a class="link" href="https://cancerprogressreport.aacr.org/progress/cpr20-contents/cpr20-preventing-cancer-identifying-risk-factors/?utm_source=aacr-org&amp;utm_medium=bynumbers&amp;utm_campaign=cpr">
        Learn More
       </a>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="num">
      <div class="inner">
       <span class="title">
        20
       </span>
       <p>
        new therapeutics against cancer were approved by the FDA from August 1, 2019, to July 31, 2020
       </p>
       <a class="link" href="https://cancerprogressreport.aacr.org/progress/cpr20-contents/cpr20-turning-science-into-lifesaving-care/?utm_source=aacr-org&amp;utm_medium=bynumbers&amp;utm_campaign=cpr#spectrum">
        Learn More
       </a>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="num">
      <div class="inner">
       <span class="title">
        27.5
       </span>
       <p>
        million people are projected to be diagnosed with cancer worldwide by the year 2040
       </p>
       <a class="link" href="https://cancerprogressreport.aacr.org/progress/cpr20-contents/cpr20-cancer-in-2020/?utm_source=aacr-org&amp;utm_medium=bynumbers&amp;utm_campaign=cpr#ongoing">
        Learn More
       </a>
      </div>
     </div>
    </div>
    <span class="num-bottom-text">
     For more statistics on cancer, please visit our Cancer Progress Report
    </span>
    <a class="btn blue tall" href="https://cancerprogressreport.aacr.org/progress/cpr20-contents/?utm_source=aacr-org&amp;utm_medium=stats-button">
     Read the AACR Cancer Progress Report
    </a>
   </div>
  </section>
  <section class="footer-cta-wrap">
   <div class="container">
    <div class="inner">
     <span class="above-title">
      Thanks to Lifesaving Cancer Research
     </span>
     <span class="title">
